  19 #include <stdint.h>
  20 #include "ksc5601.h"
  21 
  22 /*
  23 egrep  '# HANGUL SYLL' < /cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/ksc/ksc5601.txt | \
  24 egrep -v '^0x[4-9AD-F]' | egrep -v '^0x..([4-9].|A0)' | \
  25 perl tab21.pl > ksc_hangul1.tb
  26 
  27 ----------
  28    $n=0;
  29    while (<>) {
  30      local($ksc, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
  31      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
  32      local($k)=hex($ksc);
  33      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 8 eq 0);
  34      ++$n;
  35      printf (" 0x%04x,", $u);
  36    }
  37    printf ("\n");
  38 ---------
  39 
  40   2350 Hangul syllables defined in KS C 5601 are assigned
  41   row 16 - row 40 (with each row having 94 pre-composed syllables).
  42 
  43   No gap exists and all of them are sorted in Unicode 2.0 in the same
  44   order as in KS C 5601 so that we can use the single table to convert
  45   between KS C 5601-1987 based encodings(EUC-KR, ISO-2022-KR)
  46   and UCS-4.
  47 
  48 */
  49

 349 /*  Mapping table between symbols defined in KS C 5601-1992
 350     and UCS-4. It's used to convert symbols in  EUC-KR, ISO-2022-KR,
 351     Johab, UHC to UCS-4.
 352 
 353 egrep '^0xA[1-C]' < /cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/ksc/ksc5601.txt | \
 354 grep -v '# HANGUL SYLLABLE' | perl tab11.pl  > ksc_sym1.tb
 355 
 356    $n=0;
 357    while (<>) {
 358      local($ksc, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
 359      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
 360      local($k)=hex($ksc);
 361      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 4 eq 0);
 362      ++$n;
 363      printf (" [0x%04x] = 0x%04x,",
 364              int(($k - 0xa1a1) / 256) * 94 + (($k - 0xa1a1) & 0xff), $u);
 365    }
 366    printf ("\n");
 367 
 368 */
 369

 625  Mapping table from UCS4 to symbols defined in KS C 5601-1987.
 626 
 627 egrep '^0xA[1-C]' /cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/ksc/ksc5601.txt | \
 628 grep -v '# HANGUL SYLLABLE' | awk '{print $2, $1}' | sort -u |
 629 perl tab12.pl > ksc_sym2.tb
 630 
 631    $n=0;
 632    print " ";
 633    while (<>) {
 634      local($ucs4, $ksc, %rest) = split;
 635      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
 636      local($k)=hex($ksc);
 637      local($ku)=int(($k - 0xa1a1) / 256) * 94 + (($k - 0xa1a1) & 0xff);
 638      local($h)=0x21+int($ku/0x5e);
 639      local($l)=0x21+int($ku%0x5e);
 640      $n++;
 641      printf (" {0x%04x, \"\\x%x\\x%x\"},", $u, $h, $l);
 642      print "\n " if $n %3 == 0;

 645
